    function googleSignInCallback(authResult) {
        
        // Successfully authorized
        // Hide the sign-in button now that the user is authorized, for example:
        if (authResult && authResult.access_token && authResult.code) {
            
            if (APP.currentView() && APP.currentView().socialPopUpWarning) {
                APP.currentView().socialPopUpWarning("");
            }
            
            var access_token = authResult.access_token;
            var code = authResult.code;
            CONSOLE.log("info", "Google Token, Code: " + authResult.access_token + " " + authResult.code);
            
            // First get the user email for possible needs later
            gapi.client.load('oauth2', 'v2', function () {
               gapi.client.oauth2.userinfo.get().execute(function (resp) {
                   var gpuid    = WS.getUser().get('gpuid');
                   if (gpuid) {
                       // Already paired...
                       APP.slackerVM.user.gpuid(gpuid);
                       if (Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login && Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login.visible()) {
                           //...was asked to login again for something
                           Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login.onGPlusLogin(gpuid, access_token, code);
                       } else {
                           // ...just load toolbar bits.
                           APP_EVENTS.notify("onGPUserData", []);    
                       }
                   } else {
                       // Not yet paired, do full login
                       gapi.client.load('plus', 'v1', function() {
                            // https://developers.google.com/+/api/latest/
                            var request = gapi.client.plus.people.get({'userId': 'me'});
                            
                            request.execute(function(resp) {
                                if (Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login && Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login.visible()) {
                                    Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login.onGPlusLogin(resp.id, access_token, code);
                                } else {
                                    // Assume pairing request from settings.
                                    com.slacker.util.social.GooglePlus.pair("POST", resp.id, access_token, code, false, function (httpStatus, data) {
                                        if (httpStatus == 200) {
                                            
                                            WS.getUser().set({gpuid : resp.id});
                                            APP.slackerVM.user.gpuid(resp.id);
                                            
                                            APP_EVENTS.notify("onGPUserData", []);
                                        }
                                    });
                                }
                            });
                        });
                    }
                });
           });
           
        } else if (authResult && authResult.access_token) {
            CONSOLE.log("info", "Google Token: " + authResult.access_token);
            //WS.getUser().set({'access_token', authResult.access_token});
            APP_EVENTS.notify("onGPUserData", []);
            
            if (APP.currentView() && APP.currentView().socialPopUpWarning) {
                APP.currentView().socialPopUpWarning("");
            }
            
        } else if (authResult['error']) {
            CONSOLE.log("error", "Google authResult error - " + authResult.error);
            // There was an error.
            // Possible error codes:
            //   "access_denied" - User denied access to your app
            //   "immediate_failed" - Could not automatially log in the user
            // console.log('There was an error: ' + authResult['error']);
            if (authResult.error != "immediate_failed ") {
                if (Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login && Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login.visible()) {
                    Toasts.getInstance().toasts.login.reset();
                }
                if (APP.currentView() && APP.currentView().socialPopUpWarning) {
                    APP.currentView().socialPopUpWarning("");
                }
            }   
        }
    }

    function onYouTubePlayerReady(playerid){
        // YT player callback
        CONSOLE.log("info", "YT player ready: " + playerid);
        if (playerid.indexOf("modalvideoplayer") > -1) {
            var player  = getPluginObject("modalvideoplayer");
            player.setVolume(PLAYER_ENGINE.getVolume());
            //player.playVideo(); // Don't autostart right away. Need to really try to make user click the button manually so it counts.
            player.addEventListener("onStateChange", "handleModalVideoStateChange");
        } else if (playerid.indexOf("ie9promoplayer") > -1) {
            var player  = getPluginObject("ie9promoplayer");
            
            if (playerid == "ie9promoplayer_download") {
                player.addEventListener("onStateChange", "handleIE9StateChangeDownload");
            }
            if (playerid == "ie9promoplayer_dragtopin") {
                player.addEventListener("onStateChange", "handleIE9StateChangePin");
            }
        }
        
    }
    function handleModalVideoStateChange(state) {
        CONSOLE.log("info", "YT player state change: " + state);
        var player = getPluginObject("modalvideoplayer");
        
        if (state == -1) {
            // Video is loaded and unstarted.  Set a timer to start within 10 sec if the user doesn't start it manually.
            setTimeout(function () {
                try {
                    player.playVideo(); 
                } catch (e) {
                    // Player is gone...too bad
                }
            }, 10000);
        }
    }

    /**
     * build and register a list of plugins this browser is supporting

    if (navigator.plugins && navigator.plugins.length > 0) {
      var pVer  = /(\d+(\.\d+)?)\s?/;
      var _ver, i;
      if (navigator.appName.indexOf("Safari") !== -1) {
          for (i=0;i<navigator.plugins.length;i++) {
            _ver    = pVer.exec(navigator.plugins[i].description);
            this.plugins[navigator.plugins[i].name]    = {
                description    : navigator.plugins[i].description,
                version        : (_ver && _ver.length > 0) ? _ver[1] : 0
            };
          }
      } else {
          for (i in navigator.plugins) {
            _ver    = pVer.exec(navigator.plugins[i].description);
            this.plugins[navigator.plugins[i].name]    = {
                description    : navigator.plugins[i].description,
                version        : (_ver && _ver.length > 0) ? _ver[1] : 0
            };
          }
      }
    } else {
        try {
            var _flash  = new ActiveXObject("ShockwaveFlash.ShockwaveFlash.10");
            if (_flash) {
                this.plugins["Shockwave Flash"]    = {
                    description    : "Shockwave Flash 10.0 or higher for Internet Explorer",
                    version        : "10.0"
                };
            }
        } catch (e) {
            // Flash not installed
        }
    }
    
    function getPluginObject(id) {
        var f;
        if (navigator.appName.indexOf("Microsoft") !== -1) {
            f = window[id];
            if (f && f[0]) {  // in IE9, window['flash_mp3'] returns an array with two elements: the object and the embed
                f = f[0];
            } 
        } else if (navigator.appName.indexOf("Opera") !== -1) {
            f    = document.getElementById(id);
        } else {
            f = document[id];
        }
        return f;
    }

    function writeRegSetting(k,v) {
        try {
            getPluginObject("flash_mp3").setRegValue(k, v);
        } catch (e) {
    
        }
    }
    function readRegSetting(v) {
        try {
           return getPluginObject("flash_mp3").getRegValue(v);
        } catch (e) {
            return null;
        }
    }
    
    function getGlobalCookie(){
        if (SL_GC) {
    		return SL_GC; // Treat global like a singleton once it's set
    	} else {
    		var flashCache = readRegSetting('RWP');
	        // Set a global cookie object for all processes to share for the state of the web player.
	        var globalCookie   = {};
	        try {
	            globalCookie = com.slacker.util.CookieJar.getCompoundCookie('RWP', '|');
	            if (!globalCookie.v) { // If a version is not present, this has never successfully launched.
	                // Rebuild cookies.
	                if (flashCache) {
	                    //alert ("From Reg: " + readRegSetting('RWP').version);
	                    globalCookie = flashCache;
	                }
	                else {
	                    // First Launch
	                    globalCookie.fl     = (new Date()).getTime();
	                    globalCookie.vol    = 50;
	                }
	            }
	            
	        } catch (e) {
	            // 
	        }
	        // Set current version and expiry
	        globalCookie.v        = APP_VERSION;
	        globalCookie.exp     = (365 * 24 * 60); // 1 year
	        
	        return globalCookie;
    	}
    }
    
    function setGlobalCookie() {
    // SL_GC needs to be set BEFORE this is ever called.
        com.slacker.util.CookieJar.setCompoundCookie('RWP',SL_GC,'|',SL_GC.exp,"/",COOKIE_DOMAIN,null,true);
        writeRegSetting('RWP', SL_GC);
    }

    function getModalSettings() {

    }
    function resetModalSettings() {

            writeRegSetting("DoNotShowAgain", "");
        } catch (e) {
        }

        localStorage.setItem("DoNotShowAgain", "");    
    }
    
    function playbackBeacon(name, desc, obj) {
        var protocol = (obj && obj.url) ? obj.url.substring(0,4) : "";
        
        var beaconParams = {
            desc : desc,
            url  : obj.url
        };
        
        if (protocol === "rtmp") {
            beaconParams.identip     = "";
            beaconParams.blessedRtmp = obj.blessedRtmp;
            beaconParams.hasStreamed = obj.hasStreamed;
        }
        
        var qstring    = [];
        var i;
        for (i in beaconParams) {
            if (beaconParams.hasOwnProperty(i)) {
                qstring.push(i + "=" + encodeURIComponent(beaconParams[i]));
            }
        }
        
        WS.beacon(name + "?" + qstring.join("&"));
    }
    
    /**
     * Flash player event handler.
     */
    function FlashPlayer_Event(obj) {
        if (obj) {
            switch (obj.event) {
                case "log":
                    com.slacker.util.Console.log(obj.level, "FlashPlayer_Event: " + obj.msg);
                    if (obj.msg.indexOf('ident response: ') > -1) {
                        // obj.msg: (bbi_mp3player) ident response: 68.142.104.166
                        var idx = obj.msg.indexOf('ident response: ') + 16;
                        PLAYER_ENGINE.identip = obj.msg.substring(idx);   
                    }
                break;
                case "loaded":
                     com.slacker.util.Console.log("warn", "Flash is loaded and ready");
                     haveFlash   = true;
                break;
                case "error":
                     switch (obj.type) {
                         case "InvalidStreamUrl":
                         case "TrackLoadTimeout":
                         case "TrackHang":
                         case "StreamingBlocked":
                            if (obj.type == "StreamingBlocked") {
                                APP_EVENTS.notify("onNagUser", ["network-block"]);   
                            }
                            APP_EVENTS.notify("onPlayerError", ["flash", obj.type, obj.level]);
                         break;
                         
                         default:
                            APP_EVENTS.notify("onPlayerError", ["flash", "UnknownError_" + obj.type, obj.level]);
                         break;
                     }
                break;
                case "onStatisticsInfo": /* lowercase "onStatisticsInfo"" is correct.  I'm going to start replacing the starting case of the event names..  Periodic stats updates */
                    com.slacker.util.Console.log("info", "Flash onStatisticsInfo");
                    var stats = obj.payload;
    
                    var tr = SESSION.get("lastTrack");
                    if(tr) tr.set({statistics: stats});
                    
                break;
                case "OnTrackEnd":
                     com.slacker.util.Console.log("debug", "Flash OnTrackEnd");
                     PLAYER_ENGINE.stopProgress();
                     if (WS.getUser().idleTimer.isExpired()) {
                         stop("IdleUser");
                    } else {
                        skip("end");
                    }
                break;
                case "info":
                    /*
                    type                            data
                    -----------------------------   ------
                    NetStream.Buffer.Full           Playing
                    NetStream.Play.Start            Playback started
                    NetStream.Play.Stop             Playback stopped
                    NetStream.Buffer.Empty          Buffering started
                    NetConnection.Connect.Success   Starting playback
                    NetConnection.Connect.Failed    retry
                    GettingRtmpConnection           [host]
                    FindNetConnection               [Initialize|Retry]: [host] - [path]
                    RtmpConnectionTimeout           retry
                    */
    
                    // message it
                    var conErr = null;
                    var msg = null;
                    switch (obj.type) {
                        case 'GettingRtmpConnection':
                            //msg = 'Getting RTMP Connection...';
                            SESSION.set({trackProtocol: 'rtmp'});
                        break;
                        case 'FindNetConnection':
                            //msg = 'Find Net Connection...';
                        break;
                        case 'RtmpConnectionTimeout':
                            conErr = msg = 'RTMP Connection Timeout';
                        break;
                        case 'NetStream.Buffer.Full':
                        case 'NetStream.Play.Start':
                        case 'NetStream.Play.Stop':
                        case 'NetStream.Buffer.Empty':
                        case 'NetConnection.Connect.Success':
                        case 'NetConnection.Connect.Failed':
                            if (obj.type === 'NetConnection.Connect.Failed') {
                                conErr  = "RTMP Connection Failed";
                            }
                        break;
                        default:
                        break;
                    }
                    if (msg) {
                        // SLK-1472 - This will be auto replaced by the correct data once the track starts
                        // BUT, these messages here should ONLY be things that happen PRIOR to track play starting.
                        $("player-track-name").innerHTML = $("mini-track-name").innerHTML = msg;
                    }
                    if (conErr) {
                        APP_EVENTS.notify("onPlayerError", ["flash", conErr, obj.level], "warn");
                    }
                break;
                case "warn":
                     com.slacker.util.Console.log("warn", [obj.type + " : " + obj.url]);
                     playbackBeacon("IdentFailure", "IdentFailure", obj);
                break;
            }
        } else {
            com.slacker.util.Console.log("warn", "Unknown flash event: " + obj.event);
        }
    }
    /**
     * NOTE: This is a Google recommendation for resources that need to happen RIGHT AFTER page load.
     */
    function loadCssDynamically(url, id) {
        var cb = function() {
            var l = document.createElement('link'); l.rel = 'stylesheet';
            l.href = url;
            l.id    = id;
            l.type  = "text/css";
            // Append to body at the end so overrides work.
            var h = document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0]; h.appendChild(l);
            
            try {
            	if (window.addEventListener) {
					window.removeListener(cb);
				} else {
					window.detachEvent(cb);
				}
            } catch (e) {}
            
        };
        try {
            var raf = requestAnimationFrame || mozRequestAnimationFrame ||
                        webkitRequestAnimationFrame || msRequestAnimationFrame;
            if (raf) {
                raf(cb);
            } else {
                window.addEventListener('load', cb);
            }
        } catch (e) {
            // IE...you suck.
            if (window.addEventListener) {
                window.addEventListener("load", cb);
            }
            else {
                window.attachEvent("onload", cb);
            }
        }
            
    }
</script>

<script>
    /**
     * AOL Omniture Implementation.  This is VERY different from the Slacker version
    * Omniture wrapper for AJAX
    */
    function omnitureBeacon(pageName, props, options) {
        try {
            s_265.pfxID                 = "rdo";
            s_265.pageName              = pageName;
            s_265.channel               = "us.slacker";
            s_265.mmxgo                 = true;
            s_265.linkInternalFilters   = "javascript:,aolradio.slacker.com,*.sdslacker.com";
            s_265.prop54                = "other";
            s_265.prop12                = document.URL.split('?')[0];
            // This is how we get the comScore panel URL to match the beacon.
            s_265.mmxcustom             = com.slacker.app.Partner.getComScorePanelUrl(options.comScoreView, options.comScoreName, !options.doComScorePanelRequest);
            
            for (i in props) {
                s_265[i]    = props[i];
            }
            
            if (options.mmxTitleOverride) {
                s_265.mmxtitle = "AOL Radio powered by Slacker - " + options.mmxTitleOverride;
            } else if (props.prop17) {
                s_265.mmxtitle = "AOL Radio powered by Slacker - " + props.prop17;
            } else if (props.prop1 && props.prop1 == "search") {
                s_265.mmxtitle = "AOL Radio powered by Slacker - search";
            }
            
            // Fire beacon
            s_265.t();
            
            // AOL "Datalayer" beacon
            bN.set("dL_ch", s_265.channel);
            bN.set("dL_dpt", props.prop1);
            bN.set("dL_sDpt", props.prop2); // check for double encoding.
            bN.view();
            
            // Wipe variables
            s_265.pageName              = null;
            s_265.prop12                = null;
            s_265.mmxtitle              = null;
            
            for (i in props) {
                s_265[i]    = null;
            }
            
        } catch (e) {
            try {
                CONSOLE.log("warn", "OMN API not loaded: " + pageName, e);
            } catch (e2) {
            }
        }
    }
    
    // Called on page load by Omniture.  Per AOL and OMN, ignore this event for actual logging.
    function runOmni() {}
    
    // Datalayer config
    bN_cfg = {
                // The "h" parameter whitelists this hostname for beacon initialization.
                // Note: Can be a string or an array of hostnames. Use "location.hostname" to match URL of current page
                h: location.hostname,
                view : 0,
                click : 0,
                iframes : 0
            };    
    // Omniture API setup
    s_account = (OMNI_ENV == "dev")
                ? "aolrdocbsdev,devaolsvc"
                : "aolradio,aolsvc";
    (function(){
        var d = document, sA = d.createElement('script'), sD = d.createElement('script'), h = d.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        // add omniture js file
        sA.type = 'text/javascript';
        sA.src = (location.protocol == 'https:' ? 'https://' : 'http://') + 'o.aolcdn.com/os/aol/omniture.min.js';
        h.appendChild(sA);
        // add data layer js file
        sD.type = 'text/javascript';
        sD.src = (location.protocol == 'https:' ? 'https://' : 'http://') + 'o.aolcdn.com/os/aol/beacon.min.js';
        h.appendChild(sD);
    })();
